'DAS, ME YOS NAS,

1734, LCAGS BYA'I BAR, YANG SGAM PO'I ME GLANG NAS, 287 LCAGS
BYA) BKRONGS, 5 GLANG

DAR CHU LUG LO PAS SA BDAG BYAS KYANG LCAGS BYAR BKUM, DE RJES
DE'I SRAS 'OD SRUNG SOGS

BYON ZER NA SBA BZHED GTZANG MA DANG MTHUN PAR MA ZAD MKHAS
DBANG GONG MA DAG GI GSUNGS PHAL

CHER DANG YANG 'BREL LAM SNYAM MO, ,SRONG BTZAN NAS 'OD SRUNG
BAR LUNG GIS KYANG ZIN TE, 'JAM

DPAL RTZA RGYUD LAS, DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA'I BSTAN PA 'DZIN, ,RNAM

BA YI, ,GANGS CAN RI'I NANG GNAS PA'I, ,RGYAL PO MI YI LHA ZHES

RGYAL, ,DE YANG STON PA MCHOD BYED PA'O, ,KHYU MCHOG (MANG
SRONG) KHYU MCHOG (KLUNG NAM 'PHRUL)

NE) GNON NYID DAR, ,RKANG PA'I (KHRI SRONG) 'GROS SHES BSTAN PA
YIN, ,SA SRUNG (RAL PA)

DANG NI BE'U (GLANG DAR) DANG, ,'OD LDAN NYID NI PHYI MA YIN,
,ZHES GSUNGS SO, ,DAR MA LHA

LUNG DPAL GYIS BSAD RJES RJE 'BANGS KYI GO RIM 'KHRUGS NAS LO
SUM BRGYA DANG LNGA 'DAS PA NA

HOR RGYAL JING GER GYIS RGYA NAG SOGS KYI RGYAL KHAMS CHEN POR
MNGA' BSGYUR ZHING BOD KYANG ME

STAG LOR DBANG DU BSDUS TE, DE'I RIGS BRGYUD LA GSHIN RJE CHOS
RGYAL SOGS KYI SPRUL PA RE BYUNG

NAS SKABS SU BSTAN PA'I DRI MA SEL BAR BYED PA NI, YANG RTZA
RGYUD LAS, THA MAR

'CHAR RGYAS (NYI MA 'CHAR PHYOGS BYANG SHAR) CHU LHA TE, ,KLA
KLO RNAM PA SNA TSOGS YIN, ,ZHES

PAS BSTAN NO, ,DBUS GTZANG GI GNAS SRIN PO GAN RGYAL 'DRA BAR
YOD PA'I SA DGRA'I DBANG

DANG SKABS 'GAR CHOS KHRIMS RNAM DAG ZHIG NAS RGYAL BSTAN LA
CHOS LOG DANG GRUB MTHA'

MI MTHUN PA BSRES SHING CHOS SKYONG DANG 'DRE SNA TSOGS 'DRES
MAR BSTEN PA DANG, NANG 'KHRUGS

SNGA PHYI MANG PO BYUNG DUS RTEN GSUM GSHIG CING DGE 'DUN GYI
SDE MANG PO BKRONGS PA DANG MTHU

GTAD NANG PHAN TSUN DANG GZHAN LA'ANG MANG DU BYAS PAS 'OD SRUNG
MAN CHAD DA BAR DBUS GTZANG

DER 'KHRUGS PA MANG LA DPON PHAL CHER GRIR 'CHI BA SOGS BYUNG
BA'ANG, DE NYID LAS, DE

'OG LUGS NI RNAM ZHIG CING, ,PHYI ROL SKYE DGUS NYE BAR SPYOD,
,CES PAS BSTAN NO,, ,,

BOD SPYI LA DBANG BA'I RGYAL PO (BSTAN SNUB KYI LO) MED PA'I CHU
KHYI NAS LO SUM BRGYA DANG SO

BDUN 'DAS PA'I SA PHAG LA SA SKYA PA DANG TSAL BAS HOR SE CHEN
DANG 'BRI GONG NAS MUN KHE

@18 RGYAL PO DANG PHAG GRU PAS HU LU HU'I NGO BLTAS TE SO SOR
CHAD PAS HOR DE DAG GIS KYANG DE SO SOR

MCHOD CING BDAG BYAS LA, DE LAS SA PAn DANG 'PHAGS PA KHU DPON
GYI BKA' DRIN LA BRTEN NAS LAM

'BRAS PA'I LUGS 'DZIN SA SKYA PA DAR BA DANG, SGRUB BRGYUD PA'I
LUGS 'DZIN BLA MA ZHANG RIN

PO CHE'I BKA' DRIN LA BRTEN NAS TSAL BA DAR MA GRAGS SOGS LA
KHRI DPON BYUNG PA DANG, DVAGS

PO BKA' BRGYUD PA'I GTZO BO 'GRO MGON PHAG MO GRU PA'I 'PHRIN
LAS LA BRTEN NAS SGYUR RIN

DPAL SOGS LAS 'BRI GONG RGYAS PA DANG, SPYAN SNGA RGYAL PA RIN
PO (THOG RTUG PA) CHE GRAGS

BRTZON GYI DRIN LAS DPON CHEN DU GYUR PA'I PHAG GRU RDOR RGYAL
NAS PHAG GRU'I GZHI TSUGS PA'O, ,

DE LAS SA SKYA PA LA DPON GYI LUNG LAS HOR RGYAL LAS BYUNG TSUL
NI, LCAGS BYI LA CHING GES KYI

TSA BO GUN TAN RGYAL PO'I DUS DPON DON (CHE KYA DBUS GTZANG) RTA
NAG PO DANG RGYAL SMAN GNYIS

DMAG BCAS BOD DU BTANG BAS MDO STOD SMAD SOGS CHU KHAR BOD MANG
PO BSAD NAS SHAR KONG

PO NUB BAL PO LHO SMON TSUN CHAD DBANG DU BSDUS TE RVA BSGRENG
DU SER MO BA LNGA BRGYA BSAD DE RGYAL LHA

KHANG GI GLING LOG KYANG DE DUS BYUNG ZHING SO STON SOGS SKYA
SER LNGA BRGYA'ANG BKUM, SLAR DE GNYIS

KYIS MAR RGYAL PO'I PHO BRANG NYAM NGAG STE BOD DU DGE 'DUN SDE
BKA' GDAM CHE NGO BSRUNG STAG LUNG

CHOS RJE MKHAS GZI BRJID 'BRI GONG SPYAN SNGA CHE CHOS LA SA PAn
MKHAS PAR 'DUG PAS GANG

GDAN 'DREN ZHES ZHUS PAS SA PAn SPYAN DRONGS GSUNGS PA LTAR DE
SPYAN DRANGS, DE GSHEGS

NAS DPON PO 'PHAGS PA LA GU SHR'I'I 'JA' SA'I THA MA KA DANG BOD
KYI CHOS MI RTA'I (KHAMS

STOD MDO SMAD) CHOL KHA GSUM DANG, KHYAD PAR DU YIG TSANG LAS,
'BRI PHAG RGYAM G-YA' BZANG

PA DANG, ,TSAL BA (THANG PO CHE) BYA YUL LHO 'BRUG GSUM, ,BSDEBS
PAS DBUS KYI KHRI SKOR

DRUG ,MNGA' RIS LA STOD LHO BYANG GNYIS, ,CHU MIG (SHANGS) ZHA
LU BYANG 'PHROG (GUR MDO)

BCAS, ,BSDEBS PAS GTZANG GI KHRI SKOR DRUG ,GTZANG MIN DBUS MIN
YAR 'BROG GI ,

KHRI SKOR DANG BCAS BCU GSUM MO, ,ZHES PA LTAR GYI KHRI SKOR BCU
GSUM PHUL BA NAS BZUNG STE

SA SKYA PAS DPON BYAS LA, DE YANG BLA DPON GNYIS LA DPON SAR
SH'AKYA BZANG PO DANG KUN DGA'

BZANG PO DANG ZHANG BTZUN DANG PHYUG PO SGAD DKAR BA DANG BYANG
RIN DANG KUN GZHON DANG GZHON DBANG

DANG BYANG RDOR DANG YANG LON DANG, YANG GZHON DBANG DANG LEGS
DPAL DANG SENG+GE DPAL DANG 'OD ZER

@19 SENG+GE DANG KUN DGA' RIN CHEN DANG DON YOD DPAL DANG YON
BTZUN DANG, YANG 'OD ZER SENG+GE DANG RGYAL BZANG

DANG DBANG PHYUG DPAL DANG BSOD NAMS DPAL DANG, YANG RGYAL BZANG
DANG DBANG BRTZON DANG NAM MKHA'

BSTAN PA DANG GRAGS PA RGYAL MTSAN DANG DPAL 'BUM DANG BLO CHEN
DANG GRAGS DBANG SOGS BYUNG STE,

DE YANG 'PHAGS PA LA BOD SPYI PHUL BA'I RAB BYUNG BZHI PA'I CHU
GLANG NAS SHING KHYI'I 'PHAGS

PAS BDAG MDZAD RJES SHING PHAG NAS GZHI (GZHI THOG LHA KHANG,)
RIN SGANG, DUS MCHOD BLA BRANG

BZHI'ANG) THOG PA DANG SHAR BA DANG KHANG GSAR CHE MO GSUM GYIS
LO NYER LNGA RER SH'AKYA BZANG

NAS DBANG BRTZON PAR DPON NYER GNYIS KYI BAR DU BOD SPYI'I RGYAL
PO BYAS LA, 'ON KYANG KUN

BZANG HOR GYI DANG BYANG RIN G-YOG GIS BKRONGS SHING GZHON
DBANG BUD RDOR AANG LEN GSUM

GYI RING LA 'BRI GONG PA DANG 'THAB PA'I RANG GZHAN BSTAN 'GRO
KUN LA GNOD CING, DPON SHANG

RGYAL BZANG DANG DBANG BRTZON GNYIS (TSAL PA KUN RDOR DANG BCAS)
KYI RING LA'ANG KHRI SKOR BCU

GSUM GYI DMAG YAR KLUNG DU DRANGS TE PHAG GRU'I KHRI SKOR DANG
'THAB PAS PHAG GRU RGYAL TE GTZANG

SA SKYA PAS CHOL KHA GSUM LA LUNG BSGYUR BA NYAMS SO,, ,,TSAL BA
BLA MA NI ZHANG

BRTZON GRAGS KYIS GUNG THANG GI GTZUG LAG KHANG DANG 'BUM PO
CHE'I BANG RIM BZHI MAN CHAD

BZHENGS PAR MDZAD NAS 'DAS KHAR NYE GNAS DAR MA GRAGS NI SDE
GTZUG LAG KHANG GNYIS KA'I

BDAG POR BSKOS PAS PHAN THOG CHER BYAS SHING, DE RJES DE'I RUS
DPON 'BYUNG GNAS BRTZON

'GRUS DANG 'DI'I DPON LO YE 'BYUNG GIS KYANG RIM PAR DPON GYI GO
SA BSKYANGS LA, DE'I RJES

SU MGAR RGYAL BA 'BYUNG GNAS KYI SRAS SANGS RGYAS DNGOS GRUB
DPON SA BZUNG BA NAS TSAL BA

PA'I RTZA BA LEGS PAR TSUGS SHING DE'I BU DPON RIN RGYAL DANG
DE'I BU CHE BA NYI MA SHES RAB

GNYIS KYIS SA CHEN LAS 'JA' SA BLANGS, BU GNYIS DGA' BA DES DPON
BYED DUS TSAL GYI

RGYA PHIBS SOGS BZHENGS TE BSHAD GRVA SNGAGS GRVA BTZUG CING
DE'I BU SMON LAM RDO RJE'I DUS LHA

SA'I BAR SKOR BZOS NAS JO BO DANG THUGS RJE CHEN PO'I DBU THOG
GI GSER TOG SOGS BZHENGS,

DE'I BU DRUNG CHEN KUN DGA' RDO RJES RI BO DGE 'PHEL BTAB CING
PHYIS SU KHRI DPON GYI LAS KA

GCUNG GRAGS SHES LA GTAD DE RAB TU BYUNG BA'I MING SI TU DGE
SLONG ZER ZHING, DE'I BU DGE LEGS

BZANG PO DE'I BU TRES HOR DPAL 'BYOR BZANG PO DE'I BU DGA' BDE
BZANG PO'I BAR BAS MOD KYANG

@20 SMON LAM PA'I DUS 'BANGS PHAL CHER SHOR ZHING KUN RDOR DUS
SA SKYA'I DPON RGYAL BZANG SOGS

(G-YAM BZANG PA'I) DANG BSDONGS TE PHAG GRU DANG MA MTHUN PA
LAS CHER NYAMS LA, 'ON KYANG

LO BRGYA DANG BZHI BCU NYE BAR DPON BYAS PA'O,, ,,'BRI GONG PA
NI SKYOBS PA 'JIG RTEN

MGON POS 'BRI GONG MTHIL BZUNG BA NAS GZHI TSUGS TE BLA RABS
BZHI'I BAR DU DPON GYI

LAS MA BYUNG LA, PHYIS SU SKYOBS PA'I KHU BO DKON RIN GYI BU AA
MES GRAGS RGYAL GYI SRAS

TILLI PA RDO RJE GRAGS KYIS MUN KHE RGYAL PO LAS KHRI DPON GYI
'JA' SA BLANGS PA NAS RIM PAR

DPON BYAS PA'I SGOM PA RNAMS NI RDO RJE SENG+GE DANG SH'AKYA RIN
CHEN DANG BYANG CHUB DANG SPANG RAS DANG

CHOS SENG DANG RIN SENG DANG SGOM PA DPON PO DANG SH'AKYA DAR
DANG RIN GRAGS DANG YE DPAL DANG

RIN RDOR DANG KUN RIN (PHAG GRU LA NGAN SHOM) DANG SH'AKYA BZANG
DANG RJOD JI BA BSOD RIN DANG SKU

ZHANG TSUL RGYAL RNAMS BYUNG, DE RJES CHOS RGYAL DPAL BZANG NAS
BZUNG BLA DPON SBRAGS SHING

DE'I SRAS BCO LNGA RIN PO CHE'ANG GO SAR BYON, DE'I BU CHOS RJES
KUN RIN PA'I DUS SNGAR DGE

LDAN DANG 'BRI GONG BA 'BREL ZAB PA'I BSHIG STE 'BRI GONG PA'I
MNGA' 'OG GI DGE LDAN PA'I

MGON GYI ZHVA MDOG MA BSGYUR SOGS SDE 'KHRUGS MANG DU BYAS, DE
RJES DPON RIN CHEN PHUN

TSOGS PAS BLA DPON SBRAGS MA BYAS PA'I RJES SU DPON SA PHAG GRU
BAS BZUNG BA YIN NO,, ,,

'ON KYANG DE DUS 'BRI GONG BDE LTAR DANG YANG SNA DGAR RTZE BAS
HOR RGYAL LAS LUNG LAS LON

NAS ZUR DPON BYAS TE SA SKYA DANG 'BREL PAS SA SKYA'I AANG LEN
'DI'I ZHAL NGO YIN ZHING SDE

BSTAN 'DZIN PA'I DUS YAR 'BROG BTZAN RDZONG BRTZIGS SHING BO
DONG BA LA'ANG BKUR STI BYED

PA'O,, ,,YANG MI NYAG RGYAL RGOD KYI BRGYUD PA GTZANG BYANG
KHA'I NGAR SENG DANG DE'I BU RDO RJE

DPAL GYI DUS SA SKYA PA DANG 'BREL ZHING DE'I BU DKON MCHOG GI
BU 'BUM SDE'I SRAS BYANG

BDAG DPON GRAGS DAR GYIS SE CHEN LAS THAM KA LUNG LAS BLANGS
SHING 'DI'I DUS SU BYA DANG

MA RING GI CHOS SDE BTAB, DE'I BU RDO RJE MGON POS KYANG SA
SKYA'I DPON CHEN BYAS SHING DE'I BU

NAM MKHA' BRTAN PAS HOR RGYAL LAS GU'I GUNG GI DANG TA DPON GU
SHR'I'I MING DANG SHEL DAM

KYANG BLANGS,, ,,DE'I BU RIN RGYAN GYI BU CHOS GRAGS DPAL BZANG
GIS SI TU CHUNG GU'I LAS

KA DANG DE'I BU RNAM RGYAL GRAGS BZANG ZHES PA'I MKHAS PA RTZOM
(MKHAS GRUB BKA' SMAN RTZIS SGRA

@22 CHA TSANG) YANG MANG BA DES TI'I SI TU'I LAS KA DANG DE'I
GCUNG DKON MCHOG LEGS PAS SHR'I'I ZI'I

TRI SA HOS KYI LAS KA BZUNG BA LA SOGS PA'I ZUR DPON KYANG BYUNG
NGO,, ,,PHAG GRU NI SNGAR

RDO RJE RGYAL POS BZUNG BA'I GDAN SA THEL DU GNAS PA DANG DPON
SAR (SNE GU GDONG DU'AM) SDE

SRID RE YOD PA'I GDAN SAR PHYIS SU YON CHEN RGYAL BA SKYABS KYI
BU SPYAN SNGA DPON SANGS RGYAS

SKYABS DANG RGYAL BA RIN PO CHE THOG RDUGS PA SOGS RIM PAR BYUNG
DUS DAR RGYAS CHE LA, DPON

SAR GDAN SA PA THOG SDUG PA'I DUS SU HOR GYI LUNG LAS KA BYANG
NAS LDAN MA SGOM BRTZON

BSKOS KYANG TSUL MTHUN MA BYUNG BAS RKANG BZHI'I DPON RDO RJE
DPAL KHRI DPON BYAS NAS GZHI

KA BCU GNYIS BRTZIG SOGS MNGA' THANG RGYAS LA, DE RJES DE'I
GCUNG GZHON RGYAN DANG YAR 'BROG

PA BYANG GZHON DANG GZHON NU YON TAN DANG, DE RJES DE'I GCUNG
GRAGS RIN PAS BLA DPON SBRAGS

TE SA SKYAR SHOR BA'I LHA SNGA GZHI KHA RNAMS TSUR BLUS, DE RJES
DE'I GCUNG RIN SKYABS KYI BU RGYAN

BZANG DANG RGYAL MTSAN SKYABS DANG TI'I SI TU BYANG CHUB RGYAL
MTSAN RNAMS 'KHOD DE, PHYI MA (KHYI

LOD SE GI GONG NGO RTZA) 'DI'I DUS SU G-YAM BZANG BAS (BAR
THENG DU) DMAG DANG GTAM GYIS LAN

'GAR PHAM KYANG PHYIS SU SA SKYA DBANG BRTZON DANG 'THAB DUS
(LHUM STENG) BLON HOR GZHON BZANG

GI DRIN LAS PHAG GRU PAS RGYAL, YANG DPON 'BRI GONG BA TSAL BA
NAM GRAGS G-YAM BZANG BA

DANG GNYAL DMAG GIS KYANG (LHUN PO RTZE) 'THAB PA BYAS KYANG
PHAG GRU RGYAL TE BOD DBUS LA

DBANG BAR BYAS, SI TU GTZANG LA SONG NAS RAB BYUNG DRUG PA'I
SHING RTA NAS GTZANG PHAL CHER YANG

MNGA' 'OG TU BCUG NAS MAR RIN SPUNGS BKOD PA BYAS SOGS SI TU'I
DUS RDZONG BCU GSUM

BRTZIGS SHING SNE'U GDONG RTZER BRDOR NAS ZHAL LCE GCOD LUGS BCO
LNGA BTZUGS SOGS MNGA'

THANG CHEN PO BYUNG LA, DE RJES 'JAM DBYANGS GU SHR'I SH'AKA
RGYAN DANG, RJE TZONG KHA PA'I BLA MA CHOS BZHI

GRAGS BYANG DAB BSOD GRAGS DANG, DE NAS SH'KA RIN DANG CHOS
RGYAL DBANG GRAGS RGYAN PHA BUS

HOR THE MUR DANG RGYA YUNG LO RGYAL POS LUNG LAS GDAN NAS DGON
DANG LHA SDE BDAG BYAS KYANG DE'I

DUS DE'I GZIMS DPON NYANG STOD SHAR KHA PA RGYAL RTZE RAB BRTAN
PAS NANG 'KHRUGS BYAS TE RGYAL

MKHAR RTZE BDAG BYAS, DE RJES CHOS LNGA GRAGS 'BYUNG DANG DE'I
BU RDO RJE NGAG GI DBANG PO BKRA SHIS

GRAGS PA SOGS (ZHVA DMAR SKU SKYE NGAG GRAGS) BYUNG ZHING DE DAG
GI DUS BLON RIN SPUNGS NAM RGYAN

@23 PA DANG HOR GZHON BZANG DANG GZHI KHA SNEL BA DPON GRAGS
DANG NAM 'BYOR RGYAL MKHAR RTZE (RAB

BRTAN) BA DANG SDE PA 'OL KHA PA BKRA RGYAN DANG YAR RGYAB PA
BZHI MDZOD DANG BYA BA KHRI DPON BKRA

BZANG DANG DGA' LDAN DMAG DPON BSOD RGYAL SOGS BYUNG LA, DE DUS
PHAG GRU SOGS LAS

'JA' SA BLANGS PA'I LHA RGYA RI PA SOGS YUL CHUNG RER DBANG PA
LA LA BYUNG NGO,, ,,DE DAG GI

SKABS SU RIN SPUNGS NOR BZANG PA MTSO SKYES RDO RJE DON YOD RDO
RJE NGAG DBANG RNAM RGYAL SOGS DANG

RIM PAR MA MTHUN PAS GTZANG DBUS KYI SDE GZAR LANGS PA'O,, ,,DE
LTA NA SA SKYA PA'I RJES

SU LO LNGAR 'KHRUGS NAS PHAG GRU BAR THOB PA'I SHING RTA NAS
SHING YOS BAR LO GYA GNYIS LA

GTZANG DBUS PHAL CHER LA MNGA' BSGYUR ZHING DE'I TSE CHU GLANG
LA YAR KLUNG CHOS 'KHOR BYUNG NGO,, ,,

MDOR NA RAB BYUNG BZHI PA'I SA PHAG LOR SA 'BRI PHAG TSAL SO SOS
HOR RGYAL SO SO'I NGO

BLTAS TE SIL BUR GYUR PA'I PHYI LOR HOR DOR RTA BYUNG NAS RVA
BSGRENG DANG RGYAL LHA KHANG GI

GLING LOG BYUNG RJES SHING 'BRUG LA SA PAn HOR YUL DU BYON NAS
LCAGS PHAG LA 'DAS PA'I

LO PHYI MAR HOR GO TAN RGYAL POS LCAGS PHAG LA MNGAGS PA'I DMAG
BOD LA 'BYOR TE MON

MKHAR MGON PO GDONG BCOM NAS MI MANG PO BSAD CING DE RJES RGYAL
CHO JO 'BAR BKRONGS SHING

YOS LA KARMA PAKshI NI HOR YUL DU BYON NAS RGYAL PO MUNG KHE'I
BLA MA MDZAD NAP SHING BYI LA

YAR BYON, RAB BYUNG LNGA PA'I ME YOS LA HOR DMAG GIS 'DAN MA RI
BA DANG ME GLANG LA ZANGS

CHEN PA DANG 'PHAGS PA GSHEGS PA'I PHYI LO LCAGS SBRUL LA SA
SKYA'I DPON KUN BZANG BSOD

NAS BYA ROG RDZONG BCOM, DE NAS LO LNGAR SHING BYAR 'BRI GUNG
PA'I DMAG GIS BYA YUL DGON

SREGS TE GTZANG STON BKRONGS RJES SLAR 'BRI GUNG PA'I STOD HOR
GYI DMAG SA SKYA'I STENG DU

DRANGS KYANG SE CHEN RGYAL PO'I BU THI MUR BHO KHAS KYI DMAG
DANG SA SKYA'I AANG LEN GYI GTZANG

DMAG GIS DE BCOM STE SLAR KHRI THAMS CAD KYI DMAG SHAR DVAGS LA
SGAM PO'I BAR DU DRANGS

TE LCAGS STAG LA 'BRI GUNG GI LHA KHANG ME LA BSREGS PA SOGS
'BRI GONG GLING LOG KYANG

BYUNG ZHING MI KHRI BCOM BSAD, BYAR DVAGS KONG GSUM AE GNYA' LO
GSUM LHO BRAG YA

GSUM MON SOGS KYANG DPUNG GIS MNGA' 'OG TU BCUG PA NAS GTZANG
DBUS GNYIS BYA ROG

'UG PA'I BRTUL ZHUGS BZUNG NGO,, ,,PHAG GRU tA'I SI TU BYANG
RGYAN PAS KYANG RAB

@24 BYUNG DRUG PA'I SA GLANG NAS DBUS PHAL CHE RA DANG SHING
RTA NAS GTZAN YANG MNGA' 'OG TU BSDUS

NA SA LO BRGYAD CU LHAG SONG BA'I MJUG TU SLAR GTZANG BLON RIN
SPUNGS PAS 'BANGS GYEN

LOG TSUL GYIS RAB BYUNG BDUN PA'I SHING YOS NAS RIN SPUNGS NOR
BZANG GI BU KUN BZANG

GIS GZHI KHA RIN SPUNGS DANG DON GRUB RDO RJE BSAM GRUB RTZE
BSRUNG STE GTZANG PHYOGS BDAG

BYAS SHING, RAB BYUNG BRGYAD PA'I SA STAG LA DBUS KYI LHO (PHAG
GRU) BYANG (SNE'U PA)

NANG 'KHRUGS BYUNG NAS PHAG GRU'I GDAN SA'ANG SNE'U GDONG PAS
BDAG BYAS PA DANG, YANG

KUN BZANG GI BU RIN SPUNGS SDE PA SGAR BA DON YOD RDO RJE NI
ZHVA DMAR KARMA CHOS GRAGS RGYA

MTSES BSKUL TE DBUS SU LCAGS GLANG NAS DMAG KHRI TZAM DRANGS NAS
DGE LDAN PA'I SBYIN

BDAG SNE'U RDZONG PA BTON NAS BOD DBUS BDAG TU BZUNG YANG KHRI
SMON LAM PAS GTOR CHEN

GYI SGO NAS LAN GNYIS SU BZLOD PAR MDZAD, DE RJES LHA SA'I SHAR
DU SE 'BRAS KYI KHA

GNON DU KARMA PA NAG DMAR DGON BTAB STE SE 'BRAS RANG SHUGS KYIS
MED BAR BYAS 'DOD

DE KAR 'BRUG GIS DMAG KYANG DRANGS NAS DGE LUGS PA'I DGON CHUNG
LA LA BSGYUR ZHING

SE 'BRAS KYI MCHOD GZHI 'GA' ZHIG BLANGS PA NAS BZUNG KAR DGE
GNYIS PHA WANG DANG NYI

'OD LTAR GYUR ZHING SA RTA NAS RAB BYUNG DGU PA'I SA STAG BAR DU
SE 'BRAS KYI DGE 'DUN

PA LHA SA'I SMON LAM DU'ANG MA TSUD KYANG GONG GI ME KHYI NAS
DBUS KYI MI DBANG SNE'U

GDONG PA LA DPANG CUNG ZAD BYUNG, YANG ME BYA LA DGE 'DUN RGYA
MTSO RGYAL ME TOG THANG DU BZHUGS

SKABS PA'I GUNG PAS KONG DMAG DGE LDAN PA SNUBS CHED DU DRANGS
NAS 'OL KHA'I RDZONG PHYI BSHIGS

PAR BRTZAM DUS GRO MDA' BA NANG SO DON YOD DPUNG BCAS KYIS 'THAB
PAS BSHIG MA THUB KYANG

'BRI GUNG BAS KLUNG SHOD 'OD SNA SOGS DGE LDAN PA'I SDE DGON BCO
BRGYAD 'PHROG STE ZHVA GOS

CHOS LUGS BSGYUR, CHU GLANG LA NANG SO DGA' LDAN PAS SKYOR LUNG
SOGS SU DMAG KHYER BYAS

SOGS BOD CHUNG DBUS GTZANG DER GLANG DAR NAS BZUNG CHOS SRID KYI
KHRIMS YANG YANG LHOD

PAR 'ONG, ,GSUNGS PAS LUNG BSTAN THOG TU BABS PAS) PHYOGS RIS HA
CANG DAR DRAG LA,

PHAL CHER BLO RGOD CING DRAN RGYU MANG BA DANG KHYAD PAR DU YUL
DE'I BLA MA RAB BYUNG PA DANG SNGAGS

SPYOD ZER BA'I BLA GZUGS KHYIM PA DAG GIS RANG RANG GI BLO BZOS
LTA GRUB RE BYAS NAS DE DANG MI

MTHUN PA DANG LHAG PAR 'PHRIN LAS LA CUNG ZAD GNOD PA GZHAN
BYUNG TSE DPER NA RGYA GAR MKHAS

BAS RGYAL GSUNGS DANG RIGS PA LA MTHUN MI MTHUN DPANG PO GSUM
SOGS BZHAG NAS LUNG

RIGS KYIS BRTZOD DE BDEN PA'I RJES SU 'BRANG NAS CHOS PHYOGS SU
ZHI BAR MDZAD LTAR MI BYED PAR

RANG RANG GI SBYIN BDAG BLUN PO DAG BSKUL TE DMAG GIS DGE 'DUN
GYI SDE DANG RTEN GSUM BSHIG

LA'ANG LAS NGAN TSABS CHEN

DU PHYI ROL PA'I SNGAGS PA LTAR

MANG PO BKRONG SOGS KYIS

GYI 'THAB RTZOD MTHU GTAD

BOD KYI DPON CHUB DANG BLON

SONG NAS PHUG MI BSAM PAR

MI BDE BA MANG DU BYUNG NGO,, ,,

'KHRUGS PA DANG, CHU SPREL

MTSOS BSDUMS KYANG SLAR SHING

PHYI NANG GI RTEN 'BREL 'GRIGS

PA DANG, LHAN SKYES YE SHES MNGON DU MDZAD CING NANG GI RTZA LAM
SOGS DAG PAS NYAMS

SNANG DANG RMI LAM DU DKYIL 'KHOR GYI BDAG POS RDO RJE THEG PA'I
BSTAN PA GTAD DE

CHOS KYI RGYAL POR DBANG BSKUR PA 'DI NYID NI GONG DU SMOS PA
LTAR KHA SBYOR YAN

LAG BDUN DANG DBANG PHYUG BRGYAD KYI MNGA' BDAG TU SNGON RING MO
ZHIG NAS GYUR DU ZIN

MOD KYANG THA MAL PA'I DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN GYI ZOL GYIS DE DUS
BOD KYI RGYAL

BSTAN DRI MA CAN DU GYUR PA BSAM BZHIN DU GSO SLAD DU BYON PAR
NGES TE, DE CES

MNGON ZHE NA, SNGAR SRONG BTZAN SGAM PO'I DUS SU BOD DU BSTAN PA
BYUNG YANG BOD RANG

GI DGE 'DUN MA BYUNG BAS BSTAN PA'I GZHI RTZA DNGOS MA TSUGS LA,
DE LAS PHYIS

TZAM DU ZHI 'TSO BYON NAS SAD MI BDUN SOGS RAB TU BYUNG NAS
BSTAN PA CHES CHER

DAR DUS SU HVA SHANG ZHIG BYUNG NAS RGYAL BSTAN LA DRI MAS BSLAD
BCUG BYANG KA MA

LA SH'I LA BYON NAS DAG THE MDZAD, PHYIS SU GLANG DAR MAS BSTAN
PA SNUBS RJES

SU BLO CHEN GYI BU SLOB DANG LO CHEN GYIS SLAR GSOS KYANG SANGS
PAR RLOM PAS

RTZING CHOS MANG DU DAR BAR BYAS TSE JE BO RJE BYON TE DAG PAR
MDZAD PA NAS BKA'

GDAMS PA DNGOS KYI LTA DPYOD GTZANG YANG GZHAN CHOS LUGS MI 'DRA
BA DU MA BYUNG

NGO,, ,,DE RJES 'JAM DBYANGS LEGS CHOS PAS, THOS BSAM PA RNAMS
NI

GSUNG RAB KYI DON LA MI DPYOD PAR TSIG GI ZE 'THAB, SGOM CHEN PA
RNAMS BYING

RMUG GI LTA BAS GZER MTHO, SNGAGS PA RNAMS RIM GNYIS KYI DON MI
BSGOM

PAR LAG LEN GYI TSOGS 'TSO BA BSGRUB, RIG GNAS LA CUNG ZAD DPYOD
PA RNAMS

KYANG PHU'I GANGS RI MA MTHONG BA NAS MDA'I BYA SKYAG GIS MIG
'OL BA'I DUS,

ZHES GSUNGS PA'I THOG TU KHEL TE BOD KYI YUL GRU KUN TU THOS PA
GTZO BOR BYED

BA'I BSHES GNYEN CHEN POR RLOM PA DANG, DUR SMRIG GSAR BLANG MAN

@137 BSANG CHED DU NYEN PA MED ZER NAS CI YANG MI SNYAM PA DANG

ZHING GZHAN

GSANG SNGAGS DON DU GNYER BA MTHONG NA DE THOS BSAM MI NUS PA'I

LTAR THOS BSAM

GYI DUS SU BGEGS YIN ZER BA DANG, THOS PA BYANG MANG GIS PHA ROL

'GYED BYED GRANGS 'DREN DANG TSIG 'KHRI MANG PO TZAM BTZAL BA

ZAD DUR SMRIG GI

RGYAL MTSAN GYON PA'I RAB BYUNG YIN KYANG DE SNGAGS LA ZHUGS MA
THAG NAS CHANG MA DAG

PA'I SHA DUS MIN KHA ZAS MA BSTEN (CHANG RIGS MA STEN DUS MA

DANG 'GAL ZER NAS 'DOD YON LA LHAG PAR SRED PAS SO THAR GYI
BSLAB BYA MCHIL MA

BZHIN DOR NAS CHUNG MA BU BU MO DANG BCAS BZHIN DU GZHAN GYI SO
THAR MKHAN SLOB BYED

KYI BSHAD PA

LA SHANTI PA DANG NAG PO RDO RJE DANG DPAL RGYAN DANG MI THUB
ZLA BA DANG KU GU RI PA DANG

'DUL BYIN DANG SKYE MED RDO RJE MKHA' 'GRO MA DANG BLO BZANG
SNYING POS MDZAD PA STE

@375 NYI SHU DANG, SANGS RGYAS THOD PA LAS RA HA'I CHOS LNGA
DANG, 'JIGS MED

'BYUNG SBAS DANG PADMA MDZAD KYIS MDZAD PA STE BDUN DANG, RDO
RJE BDUD RTZI LA BHA GOS

MDZAD PA DANG GNYIS YOD, NYI SBAS DANG TA TH'A GA TA RAKshI TAS
MDZAD PA'I SGRO LA SKOR DANG,

SA RA HI BHA DRA SOGS KYI AO RGYAN SGROL SKOR DRUG SOGS DANG,
BHA BA BHA DRA'I CHOS BZHI

DANG; RAL GCIG MA'I SKOR LA RTAG PA'I RDO RJE DANG MAG PO PA
DANG SNYING RJE CHEN PO DANG

BSOD SNU YOMS PA DANG K'A MA LA SHR'I DANG dOM BHI HE RU KAS
MDZAD SOGS SO BZHI 'DIR

BKOD BYANG KHA CIG THE SOM CAN DANG LA LA RNAL BYOR CHEN PO MIN
PA'ANG YOD DO, ,

DUS 'KHOR SKOR LA DRI MED 'OD DANG, RGYAL PO PAD DKAR DANG DUS
'KHOR ZHABS

DANG N'A ROL PA DANG D'A RI KA PA DANG BRAM ZE BSOD SNYOMS PA
DANG S'A DHU PU DRA DANG ROL

PA'I RDO RJE DANG AA BA DHU TI PA DANG 'JAM DPAL DANG AA BHA
DANG BI BHU TI TZANDRA DANG DPAL

PHYAG NA RDO RJE DANG DPE MED MDZOD DANG NYI MA DPAL YE DANG SHA
BA RI DANG MI DBANG GRAGS

PA DANG DPE MED MTSO DANG SH'A KA SHR'I DANG SA MAN SHR'I DAN SA
DHU KIRTIS MDZAD PA SOGS

ZHE GSUM YOD LA, YANG MA RNYED PA GNYIS YOD ZER RO,, ,,

GNYIS PA SPYI'I CHOS SKOR GYI SGRUB THABS SKOR LA, SGRUB THABS
BRGYA RTZA DANG RGYA

MTSO GNYIS, RDO RJE GAN PA MNGON SHES CAN DANG THU BO R'A DZA HA
STI DANG H'Um MDZAD RDO RJE

DANG BSOD SNYOMS PA DANG GSER GLING PA DANG K'A MA LA SHR'I DANG
D'A RI KA PA DANG SH'A BA RI BA

DANG RIN RDOR DANG SHES RB GSANG B DANG SHA KA SHR'I DANG GNYIS
MED RDO RJE DANG TA TH'A GA T'A

RAKshI TA DANG LONGS SPYOD RDO RJE DANG H'Um KA RA DANG KLU
SGRUB KYIS MDZAD ZER BA DANG MI PHAM

SBAS BA'I THUGS RJE CHEN PO'I SGRUB THABS BRGYA RTZAD DANG, BA
RI'I SGRUB THABS

BRGYA RTZA STE BZHI BRGYA YOD DO,, ,,DKYIL CHOG SKOR LA, 'JIGS

MED 'BYUNG SBAS PA'I 'PHRENG BA SKOR GSUM DANG, YANG SANGS RGYAS
GSANG BA DANG

PADMA DANG SANGS RGYAS YE SHES 'JAM GRAGS DANG MEE TRI PA DANG
DGA' SKYONG DANG

RIGS SHING TU DGA' BA DANG KU RU R'A DZA DANG DPA' BO RDO RJE
DANG SHER GSANG DANG MCHOG SDE

DANG 'PHAGS PA DRA BI TA DANG KLU SGRUB DANG AIN DRA BHO DHI
DANG BI TA PA TAS MDZAD PA

@376 RNAMS DANG, SNGAGS KYI LAM RIM SOGS SNA TSOGS LA DZNY'A NA
KA RA DANG TRI PI TA KA MA

LA DANG ZHI 'TSO DANG NGAG DBANG GRAGS PA DANG PADMA BADZRA DANG
YAN LAG MED PA'I RDO RJE DANG

AINDRA BHO DHI DANG LAKshI MA DANG AA BA DHU TI PA DANG LHAN
SKYES RDO RJE DANG GNYIS RDO RJE DANG D'A

RI KA PA DANG KE RA KE PA DANG BI R'U PA DANG TEE LO PA DANG SA
RA H'A DANG TSUL KHRIMS 'PHAGS

DANG BDE BA'I RDO RJE DANG KLU SGRUB DANG MA TI TZINDRA DANG dOM
BHI BA DANG MEE TRI RJE DANG DPAL

DANG RTZA MI SANGS GRAGS DANG BDZRA P'A nI DANG TOG TZE PA DANG
SKAL BZANG RDO RJE DANG DPAL

MO DANG, DO HA KLU SOGS LAS RA H'A DANG GNYIS MED RDO RJE DANG
NAG PO RDO RJE DANG JO

BO RJE DANG KLU SGRUB DANG SHR'I AA NANTA DANG AARYA RDE BA DANG
MI TRA DZO KI DANG THUB PA BYIN DANG,

K'A MA LA SHR'I'I SGRAL MA DGU SKOR SOGS DANG, YANG BYAS BZANG
DANG NAG PO PA

DANG TI LI PA DANG BIR BA PA DANG YE SHES GRAGS PA DANG YE DPAL
DANG AINDRA BHU TI

DANG THO BTZUN RTZO YAG DANG SMRi TI DANG GHA YA DHA RA DANG
BADZRA P'A nI DANG tA LA KE DANG AA

BHYA DANG SHR'I GUPTA DANG LONGS SPYOD RDO RJE DANG SANGS RGYAS
GSANG BA DANG BI R'U PA DANG SU

DZA YA SHR'I BHA DRA DANG SHER GSANG DANG LE RDOR DANG THA 'GYUR
SBAS PA DANG RNAM PAR MI

RTOG PA DANG MAR ME MDZAD YE SHES DANG LAS ZHABS DANG KAM PA
LA'I YUM DANG

CHOS DBANG DANG NAG PO ZHABS DANG DPA' BO 'OD GSAL DANG RNYOG
MED RDO RJE SOGS

KYIS MDZAD PA RNAMS DANG, DAM TSIG DANG SDOM PA'I GZHUNG LA BHA
BHI LHA DANG

KLU SGRUB DANG AA BHA YA DANG LAKsHI LA MA DANG 'JAM GRAGS DANG
RGYAL LHA DANG DZNY'A NA

BI DHI DANG SGEG RDOR DANG JO BO DANG YE SHES BZANG PO DANG
SNYANG PO ZHABS KYIS MDZAD

PA RNAMS DANG, RAB GNAS SBYIN SREG TSOGS 'KHOR GTOR MA'I SKOR LA
SU MA

KI TI DANG NGAG GRAGS DANG RATNA RAKsHI TA DANG HE RU BADZRA
DANG AA BHYA DANG RAB 'JIGS RDO

RJED DANG ZLA 'OD DANG JO BO DANG KA MA LA MA H'A BADZRA DANG dO
MBHI HE RU KA DANG BZANG SBYIN DANG

TA TH'A GA T'A AKshI DANG MI 'JIGS PHYAG DANG KAM PA LA DANG
SANGS RGYAS GSANG BA

DANG DZO TI RI DANG RIN 'BYUNG SBAS PA PAD RNYOG MED RDO RJE
DANG KA MA LA RAKshI DANG KHA CHE

SH'AKA SHR'I DANG SRID GSUM RDO RJE DANG MI BSKYOD RDO RJE DANG
RDO RJE DRIL BU PA DANG DPAL

@377 MGON KLU SGRUB DANG BA LING A'A TZARYA DANG RATNA KIRTI
DANG TZANDRA GO MI DANG DZA MA RI DANG

BRAM ZE MCHOG SRED DANG AA BA DHU TI BA DANG SANGS GRAGS SOGS
KYIS MDZAD PA

RNAMS TE SNGAGS PHYOGS LA STONG BDUN BRGYAN ZHE BDUN DANG, SNGAR
GYI MDO PHYOGS

SKOR DANG DRIL BAS NYIS STONG SUM BRGYA BCU LHAG BOD DU 'GYUR
ZHES BU STON

GSUNGS LA, DKAR CHAG CHEN PO SOGS SU DE LAS LHAG BSHAD PA NI JO
BO'I

CHOS CHUNG BRGYA RTZA LOGS SU BGRANGS PA DANG SNGA PHYI ZLOS
SOGS KYI KHYAD PAR YIN

LA; DKAR CHAG GZHAN KHA CIG LAS DE LAS KYANG MANG DU BSHAD PA NI
SNYING SKOR

THE SOM CAN RNAMS KYANG BGRANGS PA'O,, ,,'DI DAG NI BU STON CHOS

'BYUNG DENG SNAG GRAGS CHE BAS DE LTAR BKOD PA YIN LA, 'ON KYANG
MKHAS GRUB

RJE SOGS KYI BZHED PA DANG MI MTHUN PA MANG STE, DES GSER 'OD
DANG SMAN BLA'I

MDO SOGS SNGAGS SU BZHED CING MDO'I RGYA CHER ROL PA 'KHOR LO
DANG PO DANG,

DKON BRTZEGS PHAL CHEN LANG GSHEGS TING 'DZIN RGYAL PO DANG
SNYING PO'I MDO

BCUR GRAGS PA LAS DGONGS 'GREL MA GTOGS PA'I DGU POS MTHAR THUG

THEG GCIG CHOS KUN BDAG MED KUN GZHI RNAM SHES MED PAR STON PAS
DE KUN

'KHOR LO BAR BAR 'DOD PAS DE'I 'GREL BA LA'ANG GONG DU BSHAD PA
DANG MI

MTHUN PA YOD LA, DGONGS 'GREL BSTAN 'CHOS KYI RIG GNAS LNGA LAS

NANG DON MDO 'GREL LA 'KHOR LO DANG PO'I 'GREL PAR BSTAN PA DANG
SPYOD PA

STON PA'I CHA GNYIS DANG, BAR PA'I 'GREL PA LA LTA BA DANG SPYOD
PA DANG LTA

SPYOD CHA MNYAM DU STON PA GSUM DANG, THA MA'I 'GREL PA LA'ANG
